<section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
<div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5 relative overflow-hidden">
<strong>Company Overview<br/><br/></strong>At Motorola Solutions, we're guided by a shared purpose - helping people be their best in the moments that matter - and we live up to our purpose every day by solving for safer. Because people can only be their best when they not only feel safe, but are safe. We're solving for safer by building the best possible technologies across every part of our safety and security ecosystem. That's mission-critical communications devices and networks, AI-powered video security &amp; access control and the ability to unite voice, video and data in a single command center view. We're solving for safer by connecting public safety agencies and enterprises, enabling the collaboration that's critical to connect those in need with those who can help. The work we do here matters.<br/><br/><strong>Department Overview<br/><br/></strong>As a world leader in wireless, broadband and internet technologies, Motorola Solutions is making products smarter – and life better – by unleashing the creativity of thousands of professionals from every corner of the globe.<br/><br/>The global Digital Signal Processing (DSP) team is responsible for architecting, designing and developing real-time software for digital communications and audio for Motorola Solutions worldwide portfolio two-way radio products.<br/><br/>The team is responsible for delivering Audio and RF Signal Processing Software and has ownership of all Applications Processor DSP subsystems, including Audio Management.<br/><br/><strong>Job Description<br/><br/></strong>This position is a DSP Software Engineering internship opportunity at Motorola Solutions in Plantation, Florida. We are looking for an cs or engineering major with a strong interest in DSP and embedded systems to help expand our team and deliver the next generation of communication devices to our customers.<br/><br/><strong>Responsibilities include, but are not limited to, the following:<br/><br/></strong><ul><li>Work in an Agile/Scrum team to analyze, design, implement cutting edge real-time software for DSP algorithms and Low Level device drivers to be used in wireless products. </li><li>Teamwork in a multi-site, world-wide development environment. </li><li>Finding, tracking, and repairing device software defects. </li><li>Create and execute unit, integration, system, load, and acceptance tests. <br/><br/></li></ul><strong>Preferred Skills:<br/><br/></strong><ul><li>Knowledge of fundamentals of Digital Signal Processing and/or Digital Communication. </li><li>Experience in C/C++ is a plus. </li><li>Knowledge of Machine Learning is a plus. </li><li>Experience with, Matlab, Python, Perl is a plus. </li><li>Experience in real-time embedded software is a plus. </li><li>Strong communication and problem solving skills is a plus. </li><li>Experience using version control; Git is a plus. </li><li>Experience with Linux is a plus. </li><li>Experience with embedded development/debug tools (such as emulators/JTAG, etc.) is a plus. <br/><br/></li></ul><strong>Basic Requirements<br/><br/></strong><ul><li>Candidate's graduation date must occur on or after December 2025. </li><li>Candidate must be pursuing a Bachelor’s Degree or Master’s Degree in one of the following degree programs: Computer Science, Software Engineering or Computer Engineering. </li><li>Must be a US Citizen, permanent resident or be an MS student with work authorization (F1 Visa on CPT accepted only for masters-level students). <br/><br/></li></ul><strong>Travel Requirements<br/><br/></strong>None<br/><br/><strong>Relocation Provided<br/><br/></strong>None<br/><br/><strong>Position Type<br/><br/></strong>Intern<br/><br/><em><strong>EEO Statement<br/><br/></strong></em>Motorola Solutions is an Equal Opportunity Employer. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to race, color, religion or belief, sex, sexual orientation, gender identity, national origin, disability, veteran status or any other legally-protected characteristic.<br/><br/>We are proud of our people-first and community-focused culture, empowering every Motorolan to be their most authentic self and to do their best work to deliver on the promise of a safer world. If you’d like to join our team but feel that you don’t quite meet all of the preferred skills, we’d still love to hear why you think you’d be a great addition to our team.<br/><br/>We’re committed to providing an inclusive and accessible recruiting experience for candidates with disabilities, or other physical or mental health conditions. To request an accommodation, please email ohr@motorolasolutions.com.<br/><br/>
</div>
